            function showdept(layer_ref) {		
			    
			        var a = document.getElementById(layer_ref);
			        if (document.getElementById && !document.all)
			        {			           			            
			            if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Firefox") > 0 )			            
			                {			            
			                if (a.style.visibility.length == 0)
			                    a.style.display='' ;
			                 else
			                    a.style.display = 'block' ;
			                }			            
			            else
			                {
			                if (a.style.display =='')
			                    a.style.display ='none' ;
			                else
			                    a.style.display ='';
			                 } 			          
			        }
			        else
			        {			            
			            if (a.style.display =='') {
    						a.style.display = 'none';						
						    }
					        else {
						        a.style.display='';
					        }	
			        }			        
			    }
           </script>

                <h1>
                 Chevy Truck Parts &amp; GMC Pickup Parts
                </h1>
                Searching for information on truck parts online or looking to buy
                <strong>
                 classic Chevy truck parts
                </strong>
                or GMC truck parts online? Classic Parts Of America has been the leading provider of 1947-98 Chevrolet truck parts &amp;
                <a alt="GMC Truck Parts" href="gmc_truck_parts.asp" title="Find 1947-98 GMC Truck Parts">
                 GMC truck parts
                </a>
                since 1984.    Classic Parts has an extensive inventory of Chevy parts, reproduction parts and performance
                <a alt="Pickup Truck Parts" href="pickup_truck_parts.asp" title="Find 1947-98 Pickup Truck Parts">
                 pickup parts
                </a>
                for Chevrolet trucks and GMC trucks.   We also carry 1967-1969
                <a alt="camaro parts" href="camaro_parts.asp" title="Find 1967-69 Camaro Parts">
                 Camaro parts
                </a>
                and all kinds of classic truck accessories.
                <p>
                 We have almost everything you would ever need when it comes to finding that one last classic
                 <strong>
                  Chevrolet truck part
                 </strong>
                 to complete your pickup truck renovation or restoration. Browse our website and take advantage of our online resources, such as our huge inventory of parts for Chevy trucks and our fast delivery service options. The majority of all ClassicParts.com orders placed by 2:00 p.m. (CST) are shipped the same day. ClassicParts.com removes all roadblocks when it comes to finding high-quality aftermarket GMC and Chevrolet parts.
Be sure to sign up for our newsletter and visit our popular Classic Parts Talk forum.
                </p>
               </td>
              </tr>
